msg:It took me a long time to choose a hotel this time in Beijing. Because I was traveling as a family with children, the convenience of the hotel location, the size of the hotel room and bed, and the hotel's service level were the primary factors to consider. JW Marriott Hotel Guangdong is located in Xicheng District. About 200-300 meters next to the hotel are Xuanwumen Subway Station and Caishikou Subway Station, which are convenient to various scenic spots and Universal Studios. The hotel's facilities are very complete, including restaurants, gyms and swimming pools. The room area is much larger than other budget and comfortable hotels, and children also have certain space for activities in the room. The decoration inside the room is a bit old, but Marriott has done a good job in upkeep and maintenance. The family is satisfied with the decoration and facilities. Special praise should be given to the room cleaning service. We have children staying in the hotel and the room will be messed up every day. But when we come back at night, the room service staff will always make the room very clean and even the slippers will be placed neatly. The overall service level of the hotel is in line with the standards of the Marriott brand. Every time you get off the bus at the hotel, there will always be hotel staff who will open the door and pick up your luggage for you. This is very friendly for guests with children and luggage. Mark at the front desk and I are very close. He helped us handle the procedures on the day of check-in and check-out. The whole process was very kind and efficient, and he explained the facilities and tips in the hotel in great detail. Our family stayed at Marriott for 6 nights this time. We rated Marriott quite highly and we look forward to meeting Marriott next time.
